< text>
The Mardi Gras is a nice local dive bar w/ live music a couple times a week. A couple pool tables, a decent jukebox, wise cracking bartenders and occasionally some really good free food makes the Mardi Gras a classic neighborhood corner bar. (Only  It's not on a corner). The kind of place where you don't care if anyone knows your name.</text>

<Review>Read about this spot online so had to check it out. We came at around 7pm on Saturday and were immediately seated. They have about 4-5 tables inside that are spaced out well but we got seated in the patio which also has about 4 tables. My gf and i ordered the salmon karaage for an appetizer, katsu fillet, and katsu curry. The salmon karaage was amazing. The soup broth was rich and loaded with flavor and the salmon skin was some of the best I've ever tasted. My katsu fillet was average. The panko breading was great but the fillet itself was a bit dry. If I had to do it over again I would've ordered the katsu curry instead (like my much smarter gf). That curry sauce was done very well with a hint of spice to kick up the taste buds. The service staff was extremely attentive and friendly. I will definitely be coming back to try out the other menu items soon and suggest you do the same!<//Review>< date>

< review>
I am a 47, relatively fit, guy who has never really spent much time inside of a gym up until now. My past routine of keeping active had been logging miles on the treadmill but I had always felt the need to do something more. I had a few goals in mind which included increasing overall strength, adding lean muscle, and of course losing those last few stubborn pounds around my mid-section. Having no previous background in strength training I spent a lot of time reading Men's Health magazines and watching Youtube videos but quickly became overwhelmed by a wealth of conflicting information. I just wanted to learn which workouts would be benefit my body type the most and more importantly how to perform those workouts using proper form and technique. Soon after, I decided I would benefit from some one-on-one coaching. Fortunately, I found OCFitness Coach and quickly scheduled my first meeting with Dan and Taran who both seemed genuinely interested in helping me achieve my fitness goals right from the start.

Fast-forward three months later to now. I have definitely made progress toward my goals as I am not only feeling stronger but have noticed new muscle growth which is apparent by the fact that my clothes fit better, particularly around my chest, shoulders, and arms! My posture has improved significantly as well. Some other health benefits I have noticed is that I sleep better. I had been dealing with some lingering health issues going back to last year which included morning and afternoon fatigue, insomnia, and even occasional anxiety which thanks to the work I've put in at OCFitness Coach have all mostly been resolved. I'm happy to say I am feeling great of late. I'm also getting complements from friends and co-workers who have noticed this positive change.

Regarding the actual workouts, they are challenging, but a lot of fun. And I particularly enjoy the diverse approaches of all the coaches there. As well, I never thought I would enjoy Jiu-jitsu and boxing as much as I have! It's never the same workout over and over, Dan and his team of coaches always keep it interesting. I also enjoy the end of workout discussions on things like nutrition, sleep, stress, water intake, and other physical activities. These discussions help keep me on track when I'm not at the gym.

OCFitness Coach has been an awesome experience for me personally and by far the single best life change I've made in quite some time. There aren't any egos or pretentiousness going on here, just knowledgeable fitness coaches who are genuinely interested in helping you achieve your fitness goals.< /review>

The best item I enjoyed at Moles De Los Reyes was their tortilla. Second would have to be their lamb barbacoa taco. I had the grasshopper taco and it was a tad too bitter. I would never order this again but glad I tried it.
